< review>
As a Moorpark wedding photographer (Lovisa Photo), I frequently work with many beautiful wedding venues, but Eden Gardens stands out from the rest. This wedding venue is perfect for anyone looking for an outdoor venue. The property has so many beautiful spots to photograph couples on their wedding day, and when the golden rays peek through the trees at sunset it makes for the most stunning wedding photos. If you are looking for a lush outdoor garden venue, you must check out Eden Gardens< /review>

<Name>JR Curley< /Name><time>1465773275117<//time><rating>3</rating>< review>
Although closed, the funicular railway, and the train that sits on the track, are still there, making great photo opps. In addition, historical placards provide great information on what was once a fully operational funicular. The stairs next to the tracks are still open to the public, but are in a poor state, littered with trash and the overwhelming smell of human waste.< /review>

(Translated by Google) A one-way trip costs US $ 1, a very short drive. After taking the car, I took a picture of me, and even got to the seat to get off. The retro style of the carriage is very good, you can choose to ride from bottom to top (pay when you are out of the station) or ride from top to bottom (pay when you are at the station). Because it is not expensive, it can be regarded as a scenic spot that can take pictures and ride. Although the ride is short, the route is steep and it is recommended to sit safely.

< Text>
Weekly bleachings, dime store hair cuts, 450 degree straighteners... The Spanish Inquisition's got nothing on how badly I tortured my hair. I abused it to death. No, really - the entire back was fried to straw. But i called this morning, nearly in tears and at my wits end after a bad " Super cuts" experience, and they got me in just after lunch.

So, i get there. Funky atmosphere, and original artwork on the walls. Girl at the desk is cheerful with a modern style. Exactly what you want to see going into a place like this. She offers me a beverage, all top shelf options. Such a relaxing beginning.

Then comes my stylist. Shes also quite friendly. We go through my hair and its agreed, this is a god awful mess (she was far more respectful in her phrasing but im sure she was thinking it :P ) so we talk a bit, i show some photos (always take photos with you, girls. It helps a lot!) And she sighs. Ooooooh no. Oh god. Ive been trying so hard to grow it out. Do we have to? She proceeds to gently explain what she feels is the best course of action. Ive known some doctors who could take a lesson from her about bedside manner.  I ended up agreeing to a chin length bob cut. Goodbye, shoulder length hair. I'll miss feeling you on my shoulders but this is for the best.

She was careful but not ridiculously slow. It took awhile but i think that's because she had to find a happy medium between getting all the fried hair out and not giving me a pixie cut.
An hour after i sat down, i finally got to put my glasses back on. I was stunned at how cute my hair was. The color looked real again, and the straw was all gone! At money time, she showed me the products she recommended, shook my hand, then went back to her station before i even got my card out. This is a HUGE thing for me. When a stylist hangs around, i have a hard time not feeling insanely pressured to buy the recommended products. Even if i have the same thing at home already. I found her behavior very respectful.

Walking down the street, the wind tried to screw it up, but it just couldnt.  Total Pocahontas a la disney. Stuff just kept falling right back into perfect place when the wind died down.

Its expensive. With tip, I paid 100 even. But its also typical cost for the area, and you're getting way above typical service.< /Text>

<review>I have been coming to All Creatures for 20 years for 2 dogs, and my most recent visit reminds me why.  My 14-year-old mini-dachshund suddenly became disoriented last weekend, walking in a tight clockwise circle for what seemed like an hour and having trouble finding her way home when we were out walking. I was a basket case. Dr. Mulvaney kept her at All Creatures for a few hours on Monday to observe her, and told me that it seemed to be a balance issue.  He asked me to bring her back on Thursday, and after examining her again said that she appears to have a vestibular disorder and I should watch her carefully because it often goes away by itself in 2 weeks.  Other vets might have subjected her to all kinds of tests, increasing her anxiety level.  So far, the results are bearing out the diagnosis:  she is not all better yet, but can walk or run in a straight line.  And her mood is much improved!</review></record></dataset><record>

After spending so much money and running so many tests and even doing a biopsy of her skin- the vets could not determine why she had allergies and how to fix it. We started giving her the prescription dry food the vet recommended and even medicine on a regular but nothing helped - her face continued to peal. She was very unhappy. Overall good experience with my knee MRI. Staff pretty friendly and knowledgeable. Facility very clean and modern. Total time there about 70 minutes.
Two small issues
1. I received 3 reminder notices about my appointment, all of them insisting I come 20-25 minutes early to effect a smooth check in.
